Link items I am working on to the DN

Do not (yet) use the Full Calendar plugin ^7ZiL4Fke

Only at note level (not paragraph level)
Hierarchical tags group by type and status
Used to define ExcaliBrain styles
Typifies the note:
- article
- video
- person
- meeting, etc. ^aHP9ILxM

Think of them as namespaces
Controls what gets synched with Obsidian
YouTube: starts with YYMMDD
Attachments subfolder is under folder
New files: same folder as current note ^CLdFBWj7

MoC:   _ (filename at the top of folder)
ICON:  Icon - keywords - Source
COVER: Book Cover - book title
IMAGE: Illustration - topic - Source
THUMBNAIL: Thumbnail - topic
Book on a Page: BoaP - Title
Literature Notes: LN - Title
Summary: Summary - Title
Date format YYYY-MM-DD
 ^0pUrnXi7

Based on document tags (or vice versa)
Templates to create subfolders if applicable ^gTLWY1Ph

Describes the relationship between notes
Differentiate parent/child and lateral connections
Implemented by:: DataView fields
Visualized with:: ExcaliBrain ^dRLuXhZ8

Is the entry point into a topic
Is a collection of links
For projects its typically my Storyboard ^tZa2rzUK

Link to-dos to their execution context
Add the DataView snippet to templates ^YovXzhXs

Implemented by:: Obsidian Map View
Add geo-tags to relevant notes
(i.e. holidays, workshops) ^0XFU9nYm

Atomic notes & Transclusion ^G4FnnP43

Reuse Icons (see also:: Tools/Image Library)
Deconstruct images
Use consistent sections and block references
- # Summary
- "p" for quote or other primary paragraph ^2cVHdi5J

Dynamic lists ^ubtZbWKV

Use DataView and Obsidian query to create dynamic lists
- context relevant open tasks
- vault diagnostics ^BQtrmAeU

Section Headings ^XX95cj9D

Tradeoff between atomic notes and sections
Break out sections to individual notes when
needed. Kepp it together until. ^GeGhCQIQ

Diagnostics and maintenance ^hcthXnCI

- Orphans
- "Pasted Image"  ^BZYI2bsd

Brown-field reality
